It started as an anime series in 1979 that got cancelled at around the 43 episode mark. Then in the early 80's the show became popular enough for Sunrise to do compilation films that fixed some of the animation and got rid of the more "toy-etic" attributes of the original series, so in a way they're sorta viewed as the definitive version of 0079
